              </parallelGateway>
            </branch>
            <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_functional_social'>
              <activity role='allied health or geriatric assessment team' action='assess and document pre-fracture functional ability and mobility and physical and functional level' objects='functional assessment record' id='activity_nonsurgical_functional_assessment'/>
              <activity role='allied health or geriatric assessment team' action='assess and document mental state based on pre-morbid functioning level using MMSE, MOCA, or CAM' objects='cognitive assessment record' id='activity_nonsurgical_cognitive_assessment'/>
              <activity role='allied health or geriatric assessment team' action='assess and document social circumstances including caregiver status, existing community supports, and family involvement' objects='social assessment record' id='activity_nonsurgical_social_assessment'/>
            </branch>
            <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_medication_management'>
              <activity role='pharmacist or nurse' action='complete medication reconciliation within the ED using a standardized form' objects='standardized medication reconciliation form' id='activity_nonsurgical_medication_reconciliation'/>
              <parallelGateway id='parallelgateway_nonsurgical_management'>
                <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_hydration_pain'>
                  <activity role='ED team' action='manage hydration and pain within the ED' objects='hydration treatment and pain management measures' id='activity_nonsurgical_hydration_pain_management'/>
                </branch>
                <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_delirium_pressure'>
                  <activity role='ED team' action='implement delirium prevention and pressure sore prevention measures within the ED' objects='delirium risk management and pressure sore prevention measures' id='activity_nonsurgical_delirium_pressure_management'/>
                </branch>
              </parallelGateway>
            </branch>
          </parallelGateway>
          <activity role='ED team' action='record the comprehensive baseline assessment to inform clinical decision-making, pathway trajectory, discharge planning, and performance measurement' objects='integrated hip fracture assessment record' id='activity_nonsurgical_record_baseline'/>
        </branch>
      </parallelGateway>
      <activity role='acute care team' action='admit or maintain the patient in acute care while transfer arrangements proceed' objects='bed request and ongoing monitoring plan' id='activity_nonsurgical_acute_care'/>
      <activity role='surgical hospital team' action='receive the transferred patient and perform surgery within 48 hours of the initial presentation' objects='transferred patient' id='activity_nonsurgical_surgery'/>
      <activity role='care team' action='repatriate the patient to the local hospital after surgery when appropriate' objects='postoperative transfer plan' id='activity_nonsurgical_repatriation'/>
    </branch>
  </exclusiveGateway>
</process>

[2026-07-04 22:29:13 INFO] Team leader: **[Start Chat]**

[You're a process design reviewer. Now, we share a common interest in collaborating to successfully complete a task assigned by a new customer.
You are familiar with exclusive gateway, parallel gateway and inclusive gateway in BPMN. Your main responsibilities include give suggestion to the process.
Here is a new customer's task: Module 1: Care in the Emergency Department
This module identifies recommended practices for the early assessment of suspected hip fracture
patients. Although patients typically present to the emergency department (ED), the same practices
should be followed at an outpatient clinic or when patients are directly admitted to the acute care
setting. The recommendations emphasize timely care from clinical staff and the importance of
recording a comprehensive assessment of patient factors in order to inform clinical decision-making
on the most appropriate pathway trajectory, plan discharge to the most appropriate setting and
provide baseline values for performance measurement.

Module 1 Recommended Practices
1. Care Pathway for Hip Fracture
• Every hospital should have a hip fracture care pathway that clearly specifies perioperative
  patient goals by day of stay

2. Rapid Medical Attention in the ED
• 90% of patients arriving at the ED should be seen by a physician within 1 hour
• 90% of patients should receive a consultation with an orthopedic surgeon within 2 hours
  (anesthesiologists / internist should be made aware of the patient and provide consultation as
  needed)

3. ED Assessment and Diagnostics
• Assess and document the following information while patient is in the ED to inform treatment and
  discharge decisions:
  - Reason for the fall
  - Fluid balance
  - Pressure sore risk
  - Hydration and nutrition
  - Pain
  - Temperature
  - Other collateral injuries
  - Tests for appropriate blood work
  - X-rays
  - Assess comorbid conditions
  - Current drug therapy, including any anticoagulants
  - Continence
  - Pre-fracture functional ability and mobility
  - Physical and functional level
  - Mental state based on pre-morbid functioning level, using a validated screening tool such as
    MMSE, MOCA, or CAM
  - Social circumstances, including caregiver status, existing community supports, family
    involvement

4. Patient Management Within the ED
• Medication reconciliation should be completed within the ED, using a standardized form
• Steps should be taken within the ED to manage patients' hydration, pain, risk of delirium and risk
  of pressure sores

5. Inpatient Admission
• 90% of patients should be admitted within 4 hours spent in the ED

6. Presenting to Non-Surgical Hospitals
• Patients presenting to non-surgical hospitals should be medically stabilized while waiting for
  expeditious transfer to a surgical hospital for operation
• Patients admitted to non-surgical hospitals should still receive surgery within 48 hours of their
  initial presentation
• LHINs and hospitals should ensure that all non-surgical hospitals have formal protocols for timely
  transfer to surgical hospitals for surgery, followed by repatriation to patients' local hospitals

Abbreviations: CAM, Confusion Assessment Method; ED, emergency department; LHINs, Local Health Integration Network; MMSE, Mini-Mental
State Examination; MOCA, Montreal Cognitive Assessment; SIGN, Scottish Intercollegiate Guidelines Network..
To complete the task, I will give you one or more instructions, and you must help me to write a specific solution that appropriately solves the requested instruction based on your expertise and my needs.]

  <exclusiveGateway id='exclusivegateway_hospital_capability'>
    <branch condition='presenting hospital has surgical capability' id='branch_surgical_hospital'>
      <activity role='receiving clinician' action='confirm management at a surgical-capable hospital and continue the emergency hip fracture pathway' objects='suspected hip fracture patient' id='activity_confirm_surgical_site'/>
      <parallelGateway id='parallelgateway_surgical_assessment'>
        <branch id='branch_surgical_physician'>
          <activity role='ED physician' action='see and medically assess the patient within 1 hour of arrival' objects='suspected hip fracture patient' id='activity_surgical_physician_assessment'/>
          <activity role='ED physician' action='document reason for the fall, temperature, other collateral injuries, comorbid conditions, and current drug therapy including anticoagulants' objects='patient assessment record' id='activity_surgical_physician_documentation'/>
        </branch>
        <branch id='branch_surgical_orthopedic'>
          <activity role='orthopedic surgeon' action='provide consultation within 2 hours of arrival' objects='suspected hip fracture patient' id='activity_surgical_orthopedic_consult'/>
          <activity role='ED team' action='make the anesthesiologist and internist aware of the patient' objects='patient status and consultation request' id='activity_surgical_notify_consultants'/>
          <inclusiveGateway id='inclusivegateway_surgical_consultation_need'>
            <branch condition='anesthesiology consultation is needed' id='branch_surgical_anesthesiology_needed'>

[You're a team leader. Now, we share a common interest in collaborating to successfully complete a task assigned by a new customer.
Your main responsibilities will include guiding the process design expert through process generation, process refinement, and so on.
Here is a new customer's task: Module 1: Care in the Emergency Department
This module identifies recommended practices for the early assessment of suspected hip fracture
patients. Although patients typically present to the emergency department (ED), the same practices
should be followed at an outpatient clinic or when patients are directly admitted to the acute care
setting. The recommendations emphasize timely care from clinical staff and the importance of
recording a comprehensive assessment of patient factors in order to inform clinical decision-making
on the most appropriate pathway trajectory, plan discharge to the most appropriate setting and
provide baseline values for performance measurement.

Module 1 Recommended Practices
1. Care Pathway for Hip Fracture
• Every hospital should have a hip fracture care pathway that clearly specifies perioperative
  patient goals by day of stay

2. Rapid Medical Attention in the ED
• 90% of patients arriving at the ED should be seen by a physician within 1 hour
• 90% of patients should receive a consultation with an orthopedic surgeon within 2 hours
  (anesthesiologists / internist should be made aware of the patient and provide consultation as
  needed)

3. ED Assessment and Diagnostics
• Assess and document the following information while patient is in the ED to inform treatment and
  discharge decisions:
  - Reason for the fall
  - Fluid balance
  - Pressure sore risk
  - Hydration and nutrition
  - Pain
  - Temperature
  - Other collateral injuries
  - Tests for appropriate blood work
  - X-rays
  - Assess comorbid conditions
  - Current drug therapy, including any anticoagulants
  - Continence
  - Pre-fracture functional ability and mobility
  - Physical and functional level
  - Mental state based on pre-morbid functioning level, using a validated screening tool such as
    MMSE, MOCA, or CAM
  - Social circumstances, including caregiver status, existing community supports, family
    involvement

4. Patient Management Within the ED
• Medication reconciliation should be completed within the ED, using a standardized form
• Steps should be taken within the ED to manage patients' hydration, pain, risk of delirium and risk
  of pressure sores

5. Inpatient Admission
• 90% of patients should be admitted within 4 hours spent in the ED

6. Presenting to Non-Surgical Hospitals
• Patients presenting to non-surgical hospitals should be medically stabilized while waiting for
  expeditious transfer to a surgical hospital for operation
• Patients admitted to non-surgical hospitals should still receive surgery within 48 hours of their
  initial presentation
• LHINs and hospitals should ensure that all non-surgical hospitals have formal protocols for timely
  transfer to surgical hospitals for surgery, followed by repatriation to patients' local hospitals

Abbreviations: CAM, Confusion Assessment Method; ED, emergency department; LHINs, Local Health Integration Network; MMSE, Mini-Mental
State Examination; MOCA, Montreal Cognitive Assessment; SIGN, Scottish Intercollegiate Guidelines Network..
To complete the task, I will give you one or more instructions, and you must help me to write a specific solution that appropriately solves the requested instruction based on your expertise and my needs.]

          <activity role='allied health or geriatric assessment team' action='assess and document social circumstances including caregiver status, existing community supports, and family involvement' objects='social assessment record' id='activity_surgical_social_assessment'/>
        </branch>
        <branch id='branch_surgical_medication_management'>
          <activity role='pharmacist or nurse' action='complete medication reconciliation within the ED using a standardized form' objects='standardized medication reconciliation form' id='activity_surgical_medication_reconciliation'/>
          <parallelGateway id='parallelgateway_surgical_management'>
            <branch id='branch_surgical_hydration_pain'>
              <activity role='ED team' action='manage hydration and pain within the ED' objects='hydration treatment and pain management measures' id='activity_surgical_hydration_pain_management'/>
            </branch>
            <branch id='branch_surgical_delirium_pressure'>
              <activity role='ED team' action='implement delirium prevention and pressure sore prevention measures within the ED' objects='delirium risk management and pressure sore prevention measures' id='activity_surgical_delirium_pressure_management'/>
            </branch>
          </parallelGateway>
        </branch>
      </parallelGateway>
      <activity role='ED team' action='record the comprehensive baseline assessment to inform clinical decision-making, pathway trajectory, discharge planning, and performance measurement' objects='integrated hip fracture assessment record' id='activity_surgical_record_baseline'/>
      <activity role='admitting team' action='admit 90% of patients within 4 hours spent in the ED' objects='inpatient admission order and bed request' id='activity_surgical_admission'/>
      <activity role='surgical hospital team' action='continue the inpatient hip fracture pathway toward operation' objects='admitted patient and perioperative goals by day of stay' id='activity_surgical_continue_inpatient_pathway'/>
    </branch>
    <branch condition='presenting hospital is a non-surgical hospital' id='branch_nonsurgical_hospital'>
      <activity role='receiving clinician' action='identify the non-surgical setting and initiate the transfer pathway as early as possible' objects='suspected hip fracture patient' id='activity_identify_nonsurgical_site'/>
      <parallelGateway id='parallelgateway_nonsurgical_transfer_and_assessment'>
        <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_transfer'>

            <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_stabilization'>
              <activity role='medical team' action='medically stabilize the patient while waiting for expeditious transfer to a surgical hospital for operation' objects='stabilization measures and monitoring' id='activity_nonsurgical_stabilization'/>
            </branch>
            <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_transfer_protocol'>
              <activity role='transfer coordinator and hospitals' action='activate the formal protocol for timely transfer to a surgical hospital' objects='interhospital transfer protocol' id='activity_nonsurgical_activate_transfer_protocol'/>
              <activity role='transfer coordinator and hospitals' action='arrange receiving hospital acceptance and patient transport' objects='accepted transfer request and transport arrangement' id='activity_nonsurgical_arrange_transfer'/>
              <activity role='transfer coordinator and hospitals' action='document the repatriation plan to the local hospital after surgery' objects='repatriation plan' id='activity_nonsurgical_document_repatriation'/>
            </branch>
          </parallelGateway>
        </branch>
        <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_assessment'>
          <activity role='receiving clinician' action='continue the same emergency hip fracture assessment pathway during transfer planning' objects='suspected hip fracture patient' id='activity_nonsurgical_continue_assessment'/>
          <parallelGateway id='parallelgateway_nonsurgical_assessment'>
            <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_physician'>
              <activity role='ED physician' action='see and medically assess the patient within 1 hour of arrival' objects='suspected hip fracture patient' id='activity_nonsurgical_physician_assessment'/>
              <activity role='ED physician' action='document reason for the fall, temperature, other collateral injuries, comorbid conditions, and current drug therapy including anticoagulants' objects='patient assessment record' id='activity_nonsurgical_physician_documentation'/>
            </branch>
            <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_orthopedic'>
              <activity role='orthopedic surgeon' action='provide consultation within 2 hours of arrival' objects='suspected hip fracture patient' id='activity_nonsurgical_orthopedic_consult'/>
              <activity role='ED team' action='make the anesthesiologist and internist aware of the patient' objects='patient status and consultation request' id='activity_nonsurgical_notify_consultants'/>
              <inclusiveGateway id='inclusivegateway_nonsurgical_consultation_need'>
                <branch condition='anesthesiology consultation is needed' id='branch_nonsurgical_anesthesiology_needed'>
                  <activity role='anesthesiologist' action='assess the patient and provide consultation' objects='anesthesia and perioperative risk recommendations' id='activity_nonsurgical_anesthesiology_consult'/>
                </branch>
                <branch condition='internal medicine consultation is needed' id='branch_nonsurgical_internal_medicine_needed'>
                  <activity role='internist' action='assess the patient and provide consultation' objects='medical optimization recommendations' id='activity_nonsurgical_internal_medicine_consult'/>
                </branch>
              </inclusiveGateway>
            </branch>
            <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_nursing'>
              <activity role='nursing staff' action='assess and document fluid balance, pressure sore risk, hydration and nutrition, pain, and continence' objects='ED nursing assessment record' id='activity_nonsurgical_nursing_assessment'/>
            </branch>
            <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_diagnostics'>
              <activity role='diagnostic team' action='initiate diagnostic testing for suspected hip fracture' objects='laboratory and imaging requests' id='activity_nonsurgical_diagnostic_initiation'/>

                </branch>

            </branch>
            <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_functional_social'>
              <activity role='allied health or geriatric assessment team' action='assess and document pre-fracture functional ability and mobility and physical and functional level' objects='functional assessment record' id='activity_nonsurgical_functional_assessment'/>
              <activity role='allied health or geriatric assessment team' action='assess and document mental state based on pre-morbid functioning level using MMSE, MOCA, or CAM' objects='cognitive assessment record' id='activity_nonsurgical_cognitive_assessment'/>
              <activity role='allied health or geriatric assessment team' action='assess and document social circumstances including caregiver status, existing community supports, and family involvement' objects='social assessment record' id='activity_nonsurgical_social_assessment'/>
            </branch>
            <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_medication_management'>
              <activity role='pharmacist or nurse' action='complete medication reconciliation within the ED using a standardized form' objects='standardized medication reconciliation form' id='activity_nonsurgical_medication_reconciliation'/>

                <branch id='branch_nonsurgical_hydration_pain'>

        </branch>
      </parallelGateway>
      <activity role='acute care team' action='admit or maintain the patient in acute care while transfer arrangements proceed' objects='bed request and ongoing monitoring plan' id='activity_nonsurgical_acute_care'/>

      <activity role='care team' action='repatriate the patient to the local hospital after surgery when appropriate' objects='postoperative transfer plan' id='activity_nonsurgical_repatriation'/>

  </exclusiveGateway>
</process>)</API>
